entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'migration_tool.py']
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_create_table0')

    def test_create_table(entrypoint_argv, tmp_path):
        """Core: Create a new table with basic columns."""
        migration_file = tmp_path / "migration.json"
        db_file = tmp_path / "app.db"
    
        migration = {
            "version": 1,
            "description": "Create users table",
            "operations": [
                {
                    "type": "create_table",
                    "table": "users",
                    "columns": [
                        {
                            "name": "id",
                            "type": "INTEGER",
                            "primary_key": True,
                            "auto_increment": True,
                        },
                        {
                            "name": "email",
                            "type": "TEXT",
                            "not_null": True,
                            "unique": True,
                        },
                        {"name": "name", "type": "TEXT", "not_null": True},
                    ],
                }
            ],
        }
    
        migration_file.write_text(json.dumps(migration))
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv, "migrate", str(migration_file), str(db_file)
        )
    
>       assert result.returncode == 0, f"Command failed: {result.stderr}"

                    "type": "create_table",
                    "table": "posts",
                    "columns": [
                        {
                            "name": "id",

                            "auto_increment": True,

                            "name": "created_at",

entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'migration_tool.py']
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_drop_column_preserves_exi0')

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_drop_column_preserves_existing_data(entrypoint_argv, tmp_path):
        """Functionality: Dropping a column preserves remaining data."""
        migration_file = tmp_path / "migration.json"
        db_file = tmp_path / "app.db"
    
        with sqlite3.connect(db_file) as conn:
            conn.execute(
                "CREATE TABLE customers (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, phone TEXT)"
            )
            conn.executemany(
                "INSERT INTO customers (id, name, phone) VALUES (?, ?, ?)",
                [(1, "Alice", "111"), (2, "Bob", "222")],
            )
            conn.commit()
    
        migration = {
            "version": 2,
            "description": "Drop phone column from customers",
            "operations": [
                {"type": "drop_column", "table": "customers", "column": "phone"}
            ],
        }
    
        migration_file.write_text(json.dumps(migration))
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv, "migrate", str(migration_file), str(db_file)
        )
    
>       assert result.returncode == 0, f"Command failed: {result.stderr}"
E       AssertionError: Command failed: error: Failed to spawn: `migration_tool.py`

            conn.execute(
                "CREATE TABLE users (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, first_name TEXT, status TEXT)"
            )
            conn.executemany(
                "INSERT INTO users (id, first_name, status) VALUES (?, ?, ?)",
                [(1, "alice", None), (2, "bob", None)],
            )
            conn.commit()

            "version": 2,
            "description": "Transform names then backfill matching rows",
            "operations": [
                {
                    "type": "transform_data",
                    "table": "users",
                    "transformations": [
                        {"column": "first_name", "expression": "upper(first_name)"}
                    ],
                },
                {
                    "type": "backfill_data",
                    "table": "users",
                    "column": "status",
                    "value": "'vip'",
                    "where": "first_name = 'ALICE'",
                },
            ],
        }
    
        migration_file.write_text(json.dumps(migration))

        )

_____________________ test_backfill_with_numeric_constant ______________________

entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', 'migration_tool.py']
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_backfill_with_numeric_con0')

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    def test_backfill_with_numeric_constant(entrypoint_argv, tmp_path):
        """Functionality: Backfill with numeric constant (spec: 'value can be a constant')."""
        migration_file = tmp_path / "migration.json"
        db_file = tmp_path / "app.db"
    
        with sqlite3.connect(db_file) as conn:
            conn.execute(
                "CREATE TABLE users (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, score INTEGER)"
            )
            conn.executemany(
                "INSERT INTO users (id, score) VALUES (?, ?)",
                [(1, None), (2, None)],
            )
            conn.commit()
    
        migration = {
            "version": 2,
            "description": "Backfill with numeric constant",
            "operations": [
                {
                    "type": "backfill_data",
                    "table": "users",
                    "column": "score",
                    "value": 42,  # Numeric constant
                }

    def test_add_foreign_key(entrypoint_argv, seeds_dir, tmp_path):
        """Core: Create posts table with foreign key to users."""
        migration_file = tmp_path / "migration.json"
        db_file = tmp_path / "app.db"
        shutil.copy(seeds_dir / "checkpoint_3_users.db", db_file)
    
        # First, run v1 migration to set up the version (seed already has tables)
        # Actually, the seed already has version 1, so we go directly to v2
        migration = {
            "version": 2,
            "description": "Create posts table with foreign key to users",
            "operations": [
                {
                    "type": "create_table",
                    "table": "posts",
                    "columns": [
                        {"name": "id", "type": "INTEGER", "primary_key": True, "auto_increment": True},
                        {"name": "user_id", "type": "INTEGER", "not_null": True},
                        {"name": "title", "type": "TEXT", "not_null": True},
                        {"name": "content", "type": "TEXT", "not_null": False},
                    ],
                },
                {
                    "type": "add_foreign_key",
                    "table": "posts",
                    "name": "fk_posts_user_id",
                    "columns": ["user_id"],
                    "references": {"table": "users", "columns": ["id"]},
                    "on_delete": "CASCADE",
                },
            ],
        }
    
        migration_file.write_text(json.dumps(migration))
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv, "migrate", str(migration_file), str(db_file)
        )

    def test_simple_dependency(entrypoint_argv, seeds_dir, tmp_path):
        """Core: Apply migration with dependency resolution via --migrations-dir."""
        db_file = tmp_path / "app.db"
        shutil.copy(seeds_dir / "checkpoint_5_simple_dependency.db", db_file)
    
        migrations_dir = tmp_path / "migrations"
        migrations_dir.mkdir()
    
        # Migration v1: Create users table (no dependencies)
        (migrations_dir / "migration_v1.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 1,
                    "description": "Create users table",
                    "operations": [
                        {
                            "type": "create_table",
                            "table": "users",
                            "columns": [
                                {
                                    "name": "id",
                                    "type": "INTEGER",
                                    "primary_key": True,
                                    "auto_increment": True,
                                },
                                {
                                    "name": "email",
                                    "type": "TEXT",
                                    "not_null": True,
                                    "unique": True,
                                },
                            ],
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )
    
        # Migration v2: Create posts table (depends on v1)
        (migrations_dir / "migration_v2.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 2,
                    "description": "Create posts table",
                    "depends_on": [1],
                    "operations": [
                        {
                            "type": "create_table",
                            "table": "posts",
                            "columns": [
                                {
                                    "name": "id",
                                    "type": "INTEGER",
                                    "primary_key": True,
                                    "auto_increment": True,
                                },
                                {
                                    "name": "user_id",
                                    "type": "INTEGER",
                                    "not_null": True,
                                },
                                {"name": "title", "type": "TEXT", "not_null": True},
                            ],
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )
    
        # Migration v3: Add foreign key (depends on v1 and v2)
        migration_v3 = {
            "version": 3,
            "description": "Add foreign key",
            "depends_on": [1, 2],
            "operations": [
                {
                    "type": "add_foreign_key",
                    "table": "posts",
                    "name": "fk_posts_user_id",
                    "columns": ["user_id"],
                    "references": {"table": "users", "columns": ["id"]},
                    "on_delete": "CASCADE",
                }
            ],
        }
        (migrations_dir / "migration_v3.json").write_text(json.dumps(migration_v3))
        migration_file = tmp_path / "migration_v3.json"
        migration_file.write_text(json.dumps(migration_v3))
    
        result = run_command(
            entrypoint_argv,
            "migrate",
            str(migration_file),
            str(db_file),
            "--migrations-dir",
            str(migrations_dir) + "/",
        )
    
>       assert result.returncode == 0, f"Command failed: {result.stderr}"

E       assert 2 == 0

                                    "unique": True,
                                },
                            ],
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )

        (migrations_dir / "migration_v2.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 2,
                    "description": "Add age column",
                    "depends_on": [1],
                    "operations": [
                        {
                            "type": "add_column",
                            "table": "users",
                            "column": {
                                "name": "age",
                                "type": "INTEGER",
                                "not_null": False,
                            },
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )

        (migrations_dir / "migration_v3.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 3,
                    "description": "Add name column",
                    "depends_on": [1],
                    "operations": [
                        {

                                "type": "TEXT",
                                "not_null": False,
                            },
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )
    
        # v4: Create posts table (depends on v2 and v3)
        (migrations_dir / "migration_v4.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 4,
                    "description": "Create posts table",
                    "depends_on": [2, 3],
                    "operations": [
                        {
                            "type": "create_table",
                            "table": "posts",
                            "columns": [

                                    "auto_increment": True,

                                    "name": "user_id",
                                    "type": "INTEGER",
                                    "not_null": True,
                                },

                            ],
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )
    
        # v5: Add foreign key (depends on v1 and v4)
        (migrations_dir / "migration_v5.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 5,
                    "description": "Add foreign key",
                    "depends_on": [1, 4],
                    "operations": [
                        {
                            "type": "add_foreign_key",
                            "table": "posts",
                            "name": "fk_posts_user_id",
                            "columns": ["user_id"],
                            "references": {"table": "users", "columns": ["id"]},
                            "on_delete": "CASCADE",
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )

            entrypoint_argv,
            "migrate-all",
            "--migrations-dir",
            str(migrations_dir) + "/",

    @pytest.mark.error
    def test_circular_dependency(entrypoint_argv, tmp_path):
        """Error: Detect and reject circular dependency in migration graph."""
        migrations_dir = tmp_path / "migrations"
        migrations_dir.mkdir()
    
        # Create circular dependency: 1 -> 3 -> 2 -> 1
        (migrations_dir / "migration_v1.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 1,
                    "description": "Migration 1",
                    "depends_on": [3],
                    "operations": [
                        {
                            "type": "create_table",
                            "table": "table1",
                            "columns": [
                                {
                                    "name": "id",
                                    "type": "INTEGER",
                                    "primary_key": True,
                                    "auto_increment": True,
                                }
                            ],
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )

            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 2,
                    "description": "Migration 2",
                    "depends_on": [1],
                    "operations": [
                        {
                            "type": "create_table",
                            "table": "table2",
                            "columns": [
                                {
                                    "name": "id",
                                    "type": "INTEGER",
                                    "primary_key": True,
                                    "auto_increment": True,
                                }
                            ],
                        }
                    ],
                }
            )
        )
    
        (migrations_dir / "migration_v3.json").write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "version": 3,
                    "description": "Migration 3",
                    "depends_on": [2],

                        {
                            "type": "create_table",

                            "columns": [
                                {
                                    "name": "id",

                        }

                    "version": 1,
                    "description": "Migration 1",

    @pytest.mark.error
    def test_self_dependency(entrypoint_argv, tmp_path):
        """Edge case: Migration depends on itself.

        """
        migrations_dir = tmp_path / "migrations"
